  <script>
   function setCookie(name, value, exdays) {
    var d = new Date();
    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
    var expires = 'expires=' + d.toUTCString();
    document.cookie = name + '=' + value + ';' + expires + ';path=/';
  }

  function getCookie(cname) {
    var name = cname + "=";
    var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
    var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
    for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
      var c = ca[i];
      while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
        c = c.substring(1);
      }
      if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
      }
    }
    return "";
  }

  function addVendor(vendor){
  	_vendor = vendor;
  	if(typeof window.nonIabVendorConsents == 'undefined'){
    		window.nonIabVendorConsents = [_vendor];
  	}
  	else{
  		if(!window.nonIabVendorConsents.includes(_vendor))
    		window.nonIabVendorConsents.push(_vendor);
  		}
  	setCookie("noniab_vendors",JSON.stringify(nonIabVendorConsents),90);
  }

  function getNonIabVendors(){
	  var cookie_val = getCookie("noniab_vendors");
	  if(cookie_val!="") {
	  	var noniab_vendors = JSON.parse(cookie_val);
	  }
	  return noniab_vendors;
  }

  <script>
   function checkVendor(vendorName){
    let found = false
    __cmp('getCustomVendorConsents', null, function(vendorConsents) {
      vendorConsents.consentedVendors.forEach(vendor => {
        if (vendor.name === vendorName){
          found = true
        }
      })
    })
    return found
  }

   var fingerprintReport = function () {
      Fingerprint2.get(function (components) {
        var murmur = Fingerprint2.x64hash128(components.map(function (pair) {
          return pair.value
        }).join(), 31)
        setCookie('AccessToken', murmur, 100)
      })
    }

       <a class="pink-banner" href="https://aboshop.berliner-zeitung.de" target="_blank">
        Wir sind unabhängig und wollen es bleiben. Unterstützen Sie uns dabei?

   <script>
    (function() {
    function getCookie(name) {
      var dc = document.cookie;
      var prefix = name + "=";
      var begin = dc.indexOf("; " + prefix);
      if (begin == -1) {
        begin = dc.indexOf(prefix);
        if (begin != 0) {
          return null;
        }
      } else {
        begin += 2;
        var end = document
          .cookie
          .indexOf(";", begin);
        if (end == -1) {
          end = dc.length;
        }
      }
      return decodeURI(dc.substring(begin + prefix.length, end));
    }

    function findDomain() {
      const domainArray = window
        .location
        .host
        .split('.')
      domainArray.shift()
      return domainArray.join('.')
    }

    const redirectDomain = (register) => {
      const domain = findDomain() || "berliner-zeitung.dev"
      const currentPage = window.location.href.split('?')[0]
      return `https://account.${domain}${register ? '/auth/register?rid=' + currentPage : ''}`
    };

    const loginLinkContainer = Array.from(document.getElementsByClassName("js-loginLink"));
    const loginTextContainer = Array.from(document.getElementsByClassName("js-loginText"));
    const aboshopBanner = document.getElementById('aboshop-banner');
    const aboshopBannerSmall = document.getElementById('aboshop-banner--sm');
    const separatorContainer = document.getElementById("separator-container");
    // const loginIconContainer = document.getElementById("loginIcon")
    const mppSessionId = getCookie("MPP-SessionId");
    // add class if there is session with mpp
    if(mppSessionId && document.getElementsByClassName("main-header").length > 0) {
      const mainHeader = document.getElementsByClassName("main-header")[0]
      var classString = mainHeader.className;
      var newClass = classString.concat(" logged-in");
      mainHeader.className = newClass;
      aboshopBanner && aboshopBanner.remove()
      aboshopBannerSmall && aboshopBannerSmall.remove()
      separatorContainer && separatorContainer.remove()
    }
    if (loginLinkContainer) {
      if (!mppSessionId) {
        loginLinkContainer.forEach(el => {
          el.innerHTML = `<a href="${redirectDomain(true)}" class="m-meta-navigation__link">Anmelden</a>`
        })

      } else {
        loginLinkContainer.forEach(el => {
          el.innerHTML = `<a href="${redirectDomain(false)}">Konto</a>`
        })
      }
    }
    if (loginTextContainer) {
      if (!mppSessionId) {
        loginTextContainer.forEach(el => {
          el.innerHTML = `<div class="js-loginButton">Anmelden</div>`
        })
      } else {
        loginTextContainer.forEach(el => {
          el.innerHTML = `<div class="js-logoutButton">Abmelden</div>`
        })
      }
    }
  })()
   </script>

      if (!window.doubleClickBody) window.doubleClickBody = {}
    function appendAdUnit() {
      window.unitObj = {"id":"ad-top-desktop","type":["article","page"],"target":"desktop","path":"/21876035911/disp_berliner-zeitung.de/Sport_und_Leidenschaft","divId":"div-gpt-ad-leaderboard","size":[[728,90],[970,250],[970,90]]}
      window.adClass = 'm-ad-unit--top'
      if (document.getElementsByClassName(window.unitObj.id)[0]){
        document.getElementById(window.unitObj.divId) && document.getElementById(window.unitObj.divId).remove()
        var e = document.createElement('div');
        e.id = window.unitObj.divId
        window.adClass && e.classList.add(window.adClass)
        let classList
        e.classList.add("m-ad-unit")
        classList && e.classList.add(classList)

        const script = document.createElement('script')
        script.innerHTML = `googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('${window.unitObj.divId}') });`

        e.appendChild(script)

        document.getElementsByClassName(window.unitObj.id)[0].appendChild(e)
      }
    }
    window.doubleClickBody['ad-top-desktop'] = appendAdUnit
    window.unitObj = undefined
    window.adClass = ''
     </script>

               <h2 class="m-article-teaser__title">
                Schlechtes Gewissen bleibt daheim: Urlauber starten nach Mallorca
               </h2>
               <p class="m-article-teaser__lead">
                Reisen nach Mallorca sind wieder möglich – seit Sonntag fliegt auch TUI Touristen dorthin. Hierzulande sorgt das Thema Insel-Urlaub für Streit.
               </p>

             </h2>

           </h2>
           <p class="m-article-teaser__lead">
            Ab und zu wird man nach seltsamen Begriffen gefragt. Sie klingen nach Berlin, aber man hat sie noch nie gehört. „Mopke“ ist einer davon.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="m-article-teaser__bottom">
           <span class="m-article-teaser__meta">
            Torsten Harmsen, 
  21.03.2021
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </a>

        e.appendChild(script)

      }

  <script>
   function removePlaceholders (vendor) {
      const placeholders = document.getElementsByClassName(`social-media-placeholder-${vendor}`)
      while(placeholders.length > 0) {
        document.getElementsByClassName(`social-media-placeholder-${vendor}`)[0].remove()
      }
    }

    function makeEmbedsVisible (className) {
      const embeds = document.getElementsByClassName(className)
      for (const embed of embeds) {
        embed.classList.remove('hide-embed')
      }
    }

    function fixSpacing (el) {
      const parent = el.parentNode
      parent.style.height = parent.getAttribute('data-height')
      parent.style.paddingBottom = parent.getAttribute('data-padding-bottom')
      parent.style.overflow = parent.getAttribute('data-overflow')
    }

    function enableInstagramPosts() {
      if(!document.getElementById('instagramScript')){
        makeEmbedsVisible('instagram-media')
        removePlaceholders('instagram')
        var e = document.createElement('script');
        e.id = 'instagramScript'
        e.type = 'text/javascript'
        e.async = true;
        e.src = "//www.instagram.com/embed.js";
        document.body.appendChild(e)
      }
    }

    function enableTwitterPosts() {
      if(!document.getElementById('twitterScript')){
        makeEmbedsVisible('twitter-tweet')
        removePlaceholders('twitter')
        var e = document.createElement('script');
        e.id = 'twitterScript'
        e.type = 'text/javascript'
        e.async = true;
        e.src = "https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js";
        document.body.appendChild(e)
      }
    }

    function enableTiktokPosts() {
      if(!document.getElementById('tiktokScript')){
        makeEmbedsVisible('tiktok-embed')
        removePlaceholders('tiktok')
        var e = document.createElement('script');
        e.id = 'tiktokScript'
        e.type = 'text/javascript'
        e.async = true;
        e.src = "https://www.tiktok.com/embed.js";
        document.body.appendChild(e)
      }
    }

    function enableFacebookPosts() {
      const facebookScriptUrl = '//www.facebook.com/plugins'
      for( const el of document.getElementsByTagName('iframe')) {
        if (el.getAttribute('data-src') && el.getAttribute('data-src').includes(facebookScriptUrl)) {
          el.setAttribute('src', el.getAttribute('data-src'))
          el.classList.remove('hide-embed')
          fixSpacing(el)
        }
      }
      removePlaceholders('facebook')
    }

    function enableYoutubePosts() {
      const youtubeScriptUrl = '//www.youtube.com/embed'
      for( const el of document.getElementsByTagName('iframe')) {
        if (el.getAttribute('data-src') && el.getAttribute('data-src').includes(youtubeScriptUrl)) {
          el.setAttribute('src', el.getAttribute('data-src'))
          el.classList.remove('hide-embed')
          fixSpacing(el)
        }
      }
      removePlaceholders('youtube')
    }

    function enableSpotifyPosts() {
      const spotifyScriptUrl = '//open.spotify.com/embed'
      for( const el of document.getElementsByTagName('iframe')) {
        if (el.getAttribute('data-src') && el.getAttribute('data-src').includes(spotifyScriptUrl)) {
          el.setAttribute('src', el.getAttribute('data-src'))
          el.classList.remove('hide-embed')
          fixSpacing(el)
        }
      }
      removePlaceholders('spotify')
    }

    // We have to distinguish between environments here, because we can't set up
    // Sourcepoint locally, and if we don't execute these functions, none of
    // the embeds will be shown.
    if(window.location.host.includes('localhost')) {
      enableInstagramPosts()
      enableTwitterPosts()
      enableSpotifyPosts()
      enableFacebookPosts()
      enableYoutubePosts()
      enableTiktokPosts()
    }
  </script>
